)@@G@@.ELT]                      *******  @H@@@[. *******                     RD
)@@G@@                                       *******  @H@@@[. ******* IF AN ELRE
)@@G@@T IS SPECIFIED (ELEMENT MODE), THE DESIRED         *******  @H@@@[. ****RF
)@@G@@*** ELT TYPE (S,R,A,O) CAN ALSO BE SPECIFIED IN THE OPTION     *******  RG

)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@[. ******* SEARCHED.  IF NO OPTION IS SPECIFIED, ALL ELRI
)@@G@@EMENT TYPES    *******  @H@@@[. ******* WILL BE SEARCHED.  IF VERSION OFRJ
)@@G@@ '-' IS SPECIFIED,         *******  @H@@@[. ******* ELEMENT VERSIONS WILRK
)@@G@@L NOT BE CHECKED.                      *******  @H@@@[. *******         RL
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@[. ****RM
)@@G@@*** THE CONDITION WORD WILL BE SET AS FOLLOWS:                 *******  RN
)@@G@@@H@@@[. *******                                                         RO
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@[. ******* FILE ONLY MODE      ELEMENT MODE          S6RP
)@@G@@     S5        *******  @H@@@[. ******* --------------      ------------RQ
)@@G@@          --     --        *******  @H@@@[. ******* FILE EXISTS,NOT     RR
)@@G@@ELT EXISTS            0      TYPE      *******  @H@@@[. *******   EMPTY RS
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@[. ****RT
)@@G@@*** FILE EMPTY          FILE EXISTS,ELT       1                *******  RU
)@@G@@@H@@@[. *******                       NOT THERE                         RV
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@[. ******* FILE NOT THERE      FILE NOT THERE        2 RW
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@[. *******   OR UNASSIGNABLE     OR UNASSIGRX
)@@G@@NABLE                      *******  @H@@@[. ******* FILE NOT PROG FILE  RY
)@@G@@FILE NOT PROG FILE    3                *******  @H@@@[. *******         RZ
)@@G@@                                                   *******  @H@@@[. ****SA
)@@G@@*** OPTIONS ALLOWED:                                           *******  SB
)@@G@@@H@@@[. *******                                                         SC
)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@[. ******* A,R,S,O  -- ELEMENT TYPES FOR SEARCH        SD
)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@[. ******* N        -- NO PRINT-OUTS       SE
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@[. *******                     SF

)@@G@@@H@@@[. *******                                                         SJ

)@@G@@               *******  @H@@@]. ******* 1R2  -- N OPTION ONLY DIDN'T SETSL
)@@G@@ CONDITION WORD            *******  @H@@@#. ******* 1R3  -- ADD TEST FACSM

)@@G@@OCS   @E@@@#          R$INF                       . READ INFOR TABLE    SS
)@@G@@@G@@@#          TEST                        . INVOKE TEST MODE IF @MASM,ST
)@@G@@T     @F@]@[          S         A5,OPT            . STORE PROCESSOR OPTISU

)@@G@@@F@@@[          S         A6,NOPT           . STORE AS N OPTION KEY     SW

)@@G@@          S         A7,OPT            . STORE PROCESSOR OPTIONS   @G@@@[SY

)@@G@@@ @@@[          L,S1      A0,PFPKT+6@D@@@[          S         A0,ASGKEY TI
)@@G@@        . SAVE ASG KEY  @H@@@[          JNZ       A0,CONT2          . IFTJ

)@@G@@        . ASSIGN FILE   @G@@@[          L,U       A2,2              . IFTL
)@@G@@ FAC REJECT, FILE NOT THERE   @ @@@[          JN        A0,EXIT   @G@@@[TM
)@@G@@CONT2     PFWL$P    PFPKT             . GET NEXT WRITE LOCATION OF FILE TN
)@@G@@@E@@@[          JNZ       A2,EXIT           . ABNORMAL RETURN     @F@]@[TO
)@@G@@          SZ        A2                . IF = 1792, FILE EMPTY     @ @]@[TP
)@@G@@          TNE,U     A1,1792   @F@@@]          TNE,U     A1,1792         TQ
)@@G@@  . IF = 1792, FILE EMPTY     @G@@@[          L,U       A2,1            TR
)@@G@@  . SET T3 OF CONDITION WORD TO 1   @F@@@[          TNZ       ENL       TS
)@@G@@        . WAS INPUT ELT SPECIFIED?  @D@@@[          J         EXIT      TT
)@@G@@        . NO, FINISHED  @G@@@[          DL        A0,ENAME          . MOTU

)@@G@@@I@@@[          TNZ       EVL               .   IF SPECIFIED, OTHERWISE TX
)@@G@@SET TO BLANKS     @B@@@[          DL        A0,('            ')   @H@@@[TY
)@@G@@          TE        A0,('-     ')     . IF VERSION = '-', LEAVE VERSION TZ
)@@G@@0     @ @@@[          DS        A0,PFPKT+6@G@@@[          L         X1,(UA
)@@G@@1,1)          . INITIAL PROG TYPE FOR SEARCH    @F@@@[LOOP      S,S3    UB
)@@G@@  X1,PFPKT+5        . STORE NEXT TYPE IN PACKET @G@@@[          L       UC

)@@G@@        A0,CONT3          . NO OPTIONS AT ALL   @A@@@[          TOP     UE
